As high rollers bet on who will survive, Will, his dad, and members of Will&#39;s team wage an all-out war against the game&#39;s mastermind.<br/><br/> Languages: English and Spanish.<br/><br/> Subtitles: English (Closed Captioned) and Spanish.</p> </div> <section class="js-legal-badges legal-badges"> <div class=spacer></div> <div class="js-idml-badge idml-badge Grid"> </div> </section> </section> <div class=product-specs-section> <h3>Specifications</h3> <section class="js-product-specs product-specs"> <div class="specs-table js-specs-table"> <table class="table table-striped-odd table-first-col-font-alt font-semibold"> <colgroup> <col class=table-size-fit /> <col class=table-size-fill /> </colgroup> <tbody class=main-table> <tr class=js-product-specs-row> <td>Duration:</td> <td> 111 </td> </tr> <tr class=js-product-specs-row> <td>Actors:</td> <td> Randy Orton, Eric Roberts, Wes Studi, Steven Michael Quezada, Monique Candelaria, Dylan Kenin, Alex Knight </td> </tr> <tr class=js-product-specs-row> <td>Color:</td> <td> Other </td> </tr> <tr class=js-product-specs-row> <td>Original Languages:</td> <td> English </td> </tr> <tr class=js-product-specs-row> <td>Studio &amp; Production Company:</td> <td> Lionsgate </td> </tr> <tr class=js-product-specs-row> <td>Record Label:</td> <td> Lionsgate </td> </tr> <tr class=js-product-specs-row> <td>Assembled Product Dimensions (L x W x H):</td> <td> 0.39 x 6.76 x 5.52 IN </td> </tr> <tr class=js-product-specs-row> <td>Release Date:</td> <td> 01/19/2016 </td> </tr> </tbody> </table> </div> <div class="js-show-more-trigger show-more caret"><span>Show </span></div>

guidelines">Q&amp;A tips and guidelines</a> <div class="js-question-modal-content hide-content"> <div class="qa-modal-content top-module Grid-col u-size-1"> <p class=heading-b>Q&amp;A Exchange Guidelines</p> <p>When writing your question or answer, please follow these guidelines:</p> <ul> <li>Do: Make sure your question is directly related to the product</li> <li>Do: Be specific and provide as many details as possible</li> <li>Do: Include the model number (if applicable)</li> <li>Do: Write your question in English</li> <li>Do Not: Include personal information (such as your full name)</li> <li>All submitted questions and answers are subject to the terms set forth in our Terms and Conditions</li> </ul> <p>We reserve the right not to post your question or answer if it contains any of the following:</p> <ul> <li>Any information not related to the actual merchandise or topic</li> <li>Obscenities, discriminatory language or other language not suitable for a public forum</li> <li>Advertisements or “spam” content</li> <li>Email addresses, physical addresses or other forms of contact information</li> <li>Critical or spiteful comments on other questions or answers posted on the page or their authors</li> <li>Any imagery that demonstrates incorrect use of the merchandise</li> <li>Anything that Walmart deems to be inappropriate, at Walmart&#39;s discretion</li> </ul>
